  7. upgrade_join_on_guards.base_join_only after=['predicate_pushdown.initial'] (makes guarded dim BaseJoins INNER before union dim pushdown tries to match them)
  8. union_dim_pushdown after=['predicate_pushdown.initial', 'upgrade_join_on_guards.base_join_only'] (matches settled consumer predicates and INNER dim joins)
  9. predicate_pushdown.after_union_dim after=['union_dim_pushdown'] refires_after=['union_dim_pushdown'] (only refires when union_dim_pushdown adds branch-visible dim concepts)
  10. predicate_pushdown.remove after=['predicate_pushdown.after_union_dim']
  11. merge_irrelevant_group_by.after_predicate_remove after=['predicate_pushdown.remove'] refires_after=['predicate_pushdown.remove'] (uses redundant predicates removed from grouped children)
  12. collapse_single_parent.after_pushdown after=['predicate_pushdown.remove'] refires_after=['predicate_pushdown.remove'] (a per-contributor projection becomes a bare passthrough once predicate pushdown relocates its WHERE onto the parent scan, so re-collapse it then (q81's dim-scan projection))
  13. upgrade_join_on_guards.final after=['predicate_pushdown.remove'] (uses guards moved onto joining CTEs by predicate pushdown)
  14. predicate_pushdown.after_final_upgrade after=['upgrade_join_on_guards.final'] refires_after=['upgrade_join_on_guards.final'] (HAVING-into-group push is blocked while a consumer outer-joins the group (nullable parent); rerun once the final pass has upgraded CTE-to-CTE outer joins to INNER so the relocation can fire)
  15. upgrade_outer_key_set_equivalence after=['upgrade_join_on_guards.final'] (needs upstream filters in their final position so the accumulated-filter signatures on each side are stable)
  16. simplify_null_safe_joins after=['upgrade_join_on_guards.final', 'upgrade_outer_key_set_equivalence'] (join types and CTE nullability are settled, so redundant null-safe join keys can be downgraded to =)
  17. strip_redundant_not_null after=['simplify_null_safe_joins'] (join types and CTE nullability are settled, so an IS NOT NULL on a column that no outer join can pad is tautological; runs after null-safe-join simplification, which consumes those predicates as non-null proofs)
  18. hide_unused_concepts
  19. order_inner_joins_first after=['upgrade_join_on_guards.final', 'upgrade_outer_key_set_equivalence'] (runs last so join types are final (INNER<->OUTER upgrades have settled) before INNER joins are bubbled ahead of LEFT joins)

    "premium"."_virt_presence_1717560985782532" as "_virt_presence_1717560985782532",
    "premium"."_virt_presence_9100423883841189" as "_virt_presence_9100423883841189",
    "premium"."w01_w_rev" as "w01_w_rev",
    "premium"."w01_wfname" as "w01_wfname",
    coalesce("premium"."w01_cid","premium"."w02_cid","vacuous"."w01_cid") as "w01_cid",
    coalesce("premium"."w01_cid","premium"."w02_cid","vacuous"."w01_cid") as "w02_cid"
FROM
    "premium"
    FULL JOIN "vacuous" on "premium"."w02_cid" = "vacuous"."w01_cid"),
yellow as (
SELECT
    "hard"."s02_spref" as "_virt_filter_spref_5098477653302484",
    coalesce("hard"."s02_cid","hard"."w01_cid","sedate"."s02_cid","sedate"."w02_cid") as "_virt_filter_cid_2894806887956596",
    coalesce("hard"."w01_wfname","sedate"."w01_wfname") as "_virt_filter_wfname_18483971005351"
FROM
    "hard"
    FULL JOIN "sedate" on "hard"."_virt_presence_1717560985782532" is not distinct from "sedate"."_virt_presence_1717560985782532" AND "hard"."s02_cid" is not distinct from "sedate"."w02_cid" AND "hard"."w01_wfname" is not distinct from "sedate"."w01_wfname"
WHERE
    "hard"."_virt_presence_8055547620844531" is not null
),
rambunctious as (
SELECT
    "macho"."s02_spref" as "_virt_filter_spref_8571718182910905",
    "puzzled"."w01_wfname" as "_virt_filter_wfname_2119854692870885",
    coalesce("macho"."s02_cid","puzzled"."w02_cid") as "_virt_filter_cid_9398315168254703"
FROM
    "puzzled"
    INNER JOIN "macho" on "puzzled"."w01_cid" = "macho"."s02_cid"
WHERE
    "puzzled"."_virt_presence_1717560985782532" is not null and exists (select 1 from yellow where yellow."_virt_filter_spref_5098477653302484" is not distinct from "macho"."s02_spref" and yellow."_virt_filter_wfname_18483971005351" is not distinct from "puzzled"."w01_wfname" and yellow."_virt_filter_cid_2894806887956596" is not distinct from coalesce("macho"."s02_cid","puzzled"."w02_cid"))
),
puffy as (
SELECT
    "macho"."s02_spref" as "_virt_filter_spref_408932412295862",
    "puzzled"."w01_wfname" as "_virt_filter_wfname_8573584162978190",
    coalesce("macho"."s02_cid","puzzled"."w02_cid") as "_virt_filter_cid_7120092082074110"
FROM
    "puzzled"
    INNER JOIN "macho" on "puzzled"."w01_cid" = "macho"."s02_cid"
WHERE
    "puzzled"."_virt_presence_9100423883841189" is not null and exists (select 1 from yellow where yellow."_virt_filter_spref_5098477653302484" is not distinct from "macho"."s02_spref" and yellow."_virt_filter_wfname_18483971005351" is not distinct from "puzzled"."w01_wfname" and yellow."_virt_filter_cid_2894806887956596" is not distinct from coalesce("macho"."s02_cid","puzzled"."w02_cid")) and exists (select 1 from rambunctious where rambunctious."_virt_filter_spref_8571718182910905" is not distinct from "macho"."s02_spref" and rambunctious."_virt_filter_wfname_2119854692870885" is not distinct from "puzzled"."w01_wfname" and rambunctious."_virt_filter_cid_9398315168254703" is not distinct from coalesce("macho"."s02_cid","puzzled"."w02_cid"))
),
resonant as (
SELECT
    "hard"."s02_spref" as "s02_spref",
    coalesce("hard"."s02_cid","hard"."w01_cid","sedate"."s02_cid","sedate"."w02_cid") as "s02_cid",
    coalesce("hard"."s02_cid","hard"."w01_cid","sedate"."s02_cid","sedate"."w02_cid") as "w02_cid",
    coalesce("hard"."w01_cid","sedate"."w01_cid") as "w01_cid",
    coalesce("hard"."w01_wfname","sedate"."w01_wfname") as "w01_wfname"
FROM
    "hard"
    RIGHT OUTER JOIN "sedate" on "hard"."_virt_presence_1717560985782532" is not distinct from "sedate"."_virt_presence_1717560985782532" AND "hard"."s02_cid" is not distinct from "sedate"."w02_cid" AND "hard"."w01_wfname" is not distinct from "sedate"."w01_wfname"
WHERE
    exists (select 1 from yellow where yellow."_virt_filter_spref_5098477653302484" is not distinct from "hard"."s02_spref" and yellow."_virt_filter_wfname_18483971005351" is not distinct from coalesce("hard"."w01_wfname","sedate"."w01_wfname") and yellow."_virt_filter_cid_2894806887956596" is not distinct from coalesce("hard"."s02_cid","hard"."w01_cid","sedate"."s02_cid","sedate"."w02_cid")) and exists (select 1 from rambunctious where rambunctious."_virt_filter_spref_8571718182910905" is not distinct from "hard"."s02_spref" and rambunctious."_virt_filter_wfname_2119854692870885" is not distinct from coalesce("hard"."w01_wfname","sedate"."w01_wfname") and rambunctious."_virt_filter_cid_9398315168254703" is not distinct from coalesce("hard"."s02_cid","hard"."w01_cid","sedate"."s02_cid","sedate"."w02_cid")) and exists (select 1 from puffy where puffy."_virt_filter_spref_408932412295862" is not distinct from "hard"."s02_spref" and puffy."_virt_filter_wfname_8573584162978190" is not distinct from coalesce("hard"."w01_wfname","sedate"."w01_wfname") and puffy."_virt_filter_cid_7120092082074110" is not distinct from coalesce("hard"."s02_cid","hard"."w01_cid","sedate"."s02_cid","sedate"."w02_cid"))
),
dapper as (
SELECT
    "resonant"."s02_spref" as "_virt_filter_spref_3579790197618583",
    "resonant"."w01_wfname" as "_virt_filter_wfname_8844299626133138",
    coalesce("busy"."s01_cid","resonant"."w02_cid") as "_virt_filter_cid_4716803360545490"
FROM
    "resonant"
    INNER JOIN "busy" on "resonant"."w01_cid" = "busy"."s01_cid"
WHERE
    "busy"."s01_s_rev" > 0 and exists (select 1 from yellow where yellow."_virt_filter_spref_5098477653302484" is not distinct from "resonant"."s02_spref" and yellow."_virt_filter_wfname_18483971005351" is not distinct from "resonant"."w01_wfname" and yellow."_virt_filter_cid_2894806887956596" is not distinct from coalesce("busy"."s01_cid","resonant"."w02_cid")) and exists (select 1 from rambunctious where rambunctious."_virt_filter_spref_8571718182910905" is not distinct from "resonant"."s02_spref" and rambunctious."_virt_filter_wfname_2119854692870885" is not distinct from "resonant"."w01_wfname" and rambunctious."_virt_filter_cid_9398315168254703" is not distinct from coalesce("busy"."s01_cid","resonant"."w02_cid")) and exists (select 1 from puffy where puffy."_virt_filter_spref_408932412295862" is not distinct from "resonant"."s02_spref" and puffy."_virt_filter_wfname_8573584162978190" is not distinct from "resonant"."w01_wfname" and puffy."_virt_filter_cid_7120092082074110" is not distinct from coalesce("busy"."s01_cid","resonant"."w02_cid"))
),
waggish as (
SELECT
    "macho"."s02_spref" as "_virt_filter_spref_8669387930012131",
    "puzzled"."w01_wfname" as "_virt_filter_wfname_1058454116340231",
    coalesce("macho"."s02_cid","puzzled"."w02_cid") as "_virt_filter_cid_3372101147059031"
FROM
    "puzzled"
    INNER JOIN "macho" on "puzzled"."w01_cid" = "macho"."s02_cid"
WHERE
    "puzzled"."w01_w_rev" > 0 and exists (select 1 from yellow where yellow."_virt_filter_spref_5098477653302484" is not distinct from "macho"."s02_spref" and yellow."_virt_filter_wfname_18483971005351" is not distinct from "puzzled"."w01_wfname" and yellow."_virt_filter_cid_2894806887956596" is not distinct from coalesce("macho"."s02_cid","puzzled"."w02_cid")) and exists (select 1 from rambunctious where rambunctious."_virt_filter_spref_8571718182910905" is not distinct from "macho"."s02_spref" and rambunctious."_virt_filter_wfname_2119854692870885" is not distinct from "puzzled"."w01_wfname" and rambunctious."_virt_filter_cid_9398315168254703" is not distinct from coalesce("macho"."s02_cid","puzzled"."w02_cid")) and exists (select 1 from puffy where puffy."_virt_filter_spref_408932412295862" is not distinct from "macho"."s02_spref" and puffy."_virt_filter_wfname_8573584162978190" is not distinct from "puzzled"."w01_wfname" and puffy."_virt_filter_cid_7120092082074110" is not distinct from coalesce("macho"."s02_cid","puzzled"."w02_cid")) and exists (select 1 from dapper where dapper."_virt_filter_spref_3579790197618583" is not distinct from "macho"."s02_spref" and dapper."_virt_filter_wfname_8844299626133138" is not distinct from "puzzled"."w01_wfname" and dapper."_virt_filter_cid_4716803360545490" is not distinct from coalesce("macho"."s02_cid","puzzled"."w02_cid"))
),
scrawny as (
SELECT
    "concerned"."w01_w_rev" as "w01_w_rev",
    "concerned"."w01_wfname" as "w01_wfname",
    "concerned"."w02_w_rev" as "w02_w_rev",
    "macho"."s02_s_rev" as "s02_s_rev",
    "macho"."s02_spref" as "s02_spref",
    coalesce("concerned"."w01_cid","macho"."s02_cid") as "w01_cid",
    coalesce("concerned"."w02_cid","macho"."s02_cid") as "s02_cid",
    coalesce("concerned"."w02_cid","macho"."s02_cid") as "w02_cid"
FROM
    "concerned"
    INNER JOIN "macho" on "concerned"."w01_cid" = "macho"."s02_cid"
WHERE
    exists (select 1 from yellow where yellow."_virt_filter_spref_5098477653302484" is not distinct from "macho"."s02_spref" and yellow."_virt_filter_wfname_18483971005351" is not distinct from "concerned"."w01_wfname" and yellow."_virt_filter_cid_2894806887956596" is not distinct from coalesce("concerned"."w02_cid","macho"."s02_cid")) and exists (select 1 from rambunctious where rambunctious."_virt_filter_spref_8571718182910905" is not distinct from "macho"."s02_spref" and rambunctious."_virt_filter_wfname_2119854692870885" is not distinct from "concerned"."w01_wfname" and rambunctious."_virt_filter_cid_9398315168254703" is not distinct from coalesce("concerned"."w02_cid","macho"."s02_cid")) and exists (select 1 from puffy where puffy."_virt_filter_spref_408932412295862" is not distinct from "macho"."s02_spref" and puffy."_virt_filter_wfname_8573584162978190" is not distinct from "concerned"."w01_wfname" and puffy."_virt_filter_cid_7120092082074110" is not distinct from coalesce("concerned"."w02_cid","macho"."s02_cid")) and exists (select 1 from dapper where dapper."_virt_filter_spref_3579790197618583" is not distinct from "macho"."s02_spref" and dapper."_virt_filter_wfname_8844299626133138" is not distinct from "concerned"."w01_wfname" and dapper."_virt_filter_cid_4716803360545490" is not distinct from coalesce("concerned"."w02_cid","macho"."s02_cid")) and exists (select 1 from waggish where waggish."_virt_filter_spref_8669387930012131" is not distinct from "macho"."s02_spref" and waggish."_virt_filter_wfname_1058454116340231" is not distinct from "concerned"."w01_wfname" and waggish."_virt_filter_cid_3372101147059031" is not distinct from coalesce("concerned"."w02_cid","macho"."s02_cid"))
),
charming as (
SELECT
    "scrawny"."s02_spref" as "_virt_filter_spref_2790973759491644",
    "scrawny"."w01_wfname" as "_virt_filter_wfname_1156876110096367",
    "scrawny"."w02_cid" as "_virt_filter_cid_7186477337277761"
FROM
    "scrawny"
    INNER JOIN "busy" on "scrawny"."s02_cid" = "busy"."s01_cid"
WHERE
    ("scrawny"."w02_w_rev" - "scrawny"."w01_w_rev") / "scrawny"."w01_w_rev" > ("scrawny"."s02_s_rev" - "busy"."s01_s_rev") / "busy"."s01_s_rev"
),
elated as (
SELECT
    "cool"."pref_out" as "pref_out",
    "cool"."s02_spref" as "s02_spref",
    "vast"."first_name" as "first_name",
    "vast"."w01_wfname" as "w01_wfname",
    coalesce("cool"."w02_cid","courageous"."code","vast"."w02_cid") as "code",
    coalesce("cool"."w02_cid","courageous"."w02_cid","vast"."w02_cid") as "w02_cid"
FROM
    "courageous"
    INNER JOIN "cool" on "courageous"."code" = "cool"."s02_cid"
    INNER JOIN "vast" on "cool"."s02_cid" = "vast"."w01_cid" AND "courageous"."code" = "vast"."w01_cid"
WHERE
    coalesce("cool"."w02_cid","courageous"."code","vast"."w02_cid") is not null and exists (select 1 from yellow where yellow."_virt_filter_spref_5098477653302484" is not distinct from "cool"."s02_spref" and yellow."_virt_filter_wfname_18483971005351" is not distinct from "vast"."w01_wfname" and yellow."_virt_filter_cid_2894806887956596" is not distinct from coalesce("cool"."w02_cid","courageous"."w02_cid","vast"."w02_cid")) and exists (select 1 from rambunctious where rambunctious."_virt_filter_spref_8571718182910905" is not distinct from "cool"."s02_spref" and rambunctious."_virt_filter_wfname_2119854692870885" is not distinct from "vast"."w01_wfname" and rambunctious."_virt_filter_cid_9398315168254703" is not distinct from coalesce("cool"."w02_cid","courageous"."w02_cid","vast"."w02_cid")) and exists (select 1 from puffy where puffy."_virt_filter_spref_408932412295862" is not distinct from "cool"."s02_spref" and puffy."_virt_filter_wfname_8573584162978190" is not distinct from "vast"."w01_wfname" and puffy."_virt_filter_cid_7120092082074110" is not distinct from coalesce("cool"."w02_cid","courageous"."w02_cid","vast"."w02_cid")) and exists (select 1 from dapper where dapper."_virt_filter_spref_3579790197618583" is not distinct from "cool"."s02_spref" and dapper."_virt_filter_wfname_8844299626133138" is not distinct from "vast"."w01_wfname" and dapper."_virt_filter_cid_4716803360545490" is not distinct from coalesce("cool"."w02_cid","courageous"."w02_cid","vast"."w02_cid")) and exists (select 1 from waggish where waggish."_virt_filter_spref_8669387930012131" is not distinct from "cool"."s02_spref" and waggish."_virt_filter_wfname_1058454116340231" is not distinct from "vast"."w01_wfname" and waggish."_virt_filter_cid_3372101147059031" is not distinct from coalesce("cool"."w02_cid","courageous"."w02_cid","vast"."w02_cid")) and exists (select 1 from charming where charming."_virt_filter_spref_2790973759491644" is not distinct from "cool"."s02_spref" and charming."_virt_filter_wfname_1156876110096367" is not distinct from "vast"."w01_wfname" and charming."_virt_filter_cid_7186477337277761" is not distinct from coalesce("cool"."w02_cid","courageous"."w02_cid","vast"."w02_cid"))
)
SELECT
    "elated"."code" as "code",
    "elated"."first_name" as "first_name",
    "elated"."pref_out" as "pref_out"
FROM
    "elated"
ORDER BY 
    "elated"."code" asc nulls first
LIMIT (100)
